<script type="text/javascript">  
// 几种cookie的有效时间	
ipExpireDays      = 2;  //地址cookie

var defaultBeijingGeoID = {7:10021,8:10019,9:10023,10:10020,11:10007,12:10009,13:10011,14:10013,15:10015,16:10024};

//ip
$(function(){
    var geoData = null;
    var isMu = null;
    var municipalities = {"1":{"prov":1,"city":2},"310000":{"prov":310000,"city":310100},"500000":{"prov":500000,"city":500100},"120000":{"prov":120000,"city":120100}};
    //var msg = '送货至：';
    var getPs = $.cookies.get('ps');
    var uuuuUrl = window.location.href;
    if ( (uuuuUrl.indexOf('/list') >= 0 || uuuuUrl.indexOf('/actlist') >= 0) && /-([\d]+,[\d]+,[\d]+,[\d]+)[-\.][^-]+\.html/.test(uuuuUrl) ) {
        var psParam = uuuuUrl.match(/-([\d]+),([\d]+),([\d]+),([\d]+)[-\.][^-]+\.html/);
        if( getPs!=psParam[1]+','+psParam[2]+','+psParam[3]+','+psParam[4] ){
            _intoObj.setGeos(psParam[1], psParam[2],psParam[3],psParam[4],showPsName);
        }else{
            showPsName();
        }
    }else{
        showPsName();
    }
 
    function showPsName(){
        var jsonStr = getJsonStrForGeos();
        var showStr = '';
        var i = 0;
        var beijingFlag = false;
        if(typeof jsonStr !='object'){
            jsonStr = $.parseJSON(jsonStr);
        }    
        var strArr = [];
        $.each(jsonStr,function(m,n){
            if(m == '1' || m== '310000' || m == '120000'){
                beijingFlag = true;
            }    
            strArr[i] = n;
            i++;
        });
        if(beijingFlag){
            showStr = strArr[0]+' '+strArr[2];
        }else{
            showStr = strArr[0]+' '+strArr[1];
        }
        showStr = decodeURIComponent(showStr);     
        $('.city_2013_tit strong,#city_2014 b').html(cut_str(showStr)).attr('title',showStr).attr('alt', showStr);
    }
      
    function getJsonStrForGeos(){
        var geosObj = _intoObj.getGeos();
        var geoName = _intoObj.getCurrentGeoName();
        var jsonStr = '{"'+geosObj[0]+'":"'+geoName[0]+'","'+geosObj[3]+'":"'+geoName[1]+'","'+geosObj[6]+'":"'+geoName[2]+'"}';
        jsonStr = $.parseJSON(jsonStr);
        
        $("#ttprov").val(geosObj[0]).attr('provname',geoName[0]);
        $("#ttcity").val(geosObj[3]).attr('cityname',geoName[1]);
        $("#ttdistinct").val(geosObj[6]).attr('distinctname',geoName[2]);
        $("#ttarea").val(geosObj[9]).attr('areaname',geoName[3]);

        return jsonStr;
    }
  
     // 判断是否直辖市
    function isMuni(provId) {
        if (provId in municipalities) {
            for (muniIndex in municipalities) {
                if (municipalities[muniIndex].prov == provId) {
                    return muniIndex;
                }
            }
        } else {
            return -1;
        }
    }
    function cut_str(str) {
        var len = 6;
        if (str.length > len) {
            //str = str.substr(0, len) + '...';
        }
        return str;
    }   
    // 顶部按钮
    $('.city_2013_tit img,#city_2014').bind('click',function(){
        createMask();
    });
    
    $(window).bind('resize',function(){
        var mask = $('#shadowMask');
        var ss = $('#dsdfsd');
        if(mask.length>0){
            // console.log($(document).height());
            mask.height($(document).height());// '100%';
            // mask.width($(document).width()+500);//'100%';
        }
    });
    $(window).bind('scroll',function(){
        var mask = $('#shadowMask');
        if(mask.length>0){
            // console.log($(document).height());
            mask.height($(document).height());// '100%';
            // mask.width($(document).width()+500);//'100%';
        }
    });
    // 显示蒙版
    function createMask(){
        $('<div id="shadowMask"></div>').appendTo($('body'));
        $('#shadowMask').show();
        $('#shadowMask').height($(document).height());
        $('#citySelect').css('z-index',2147483584);
        $('#citySelect').show();
        $(window).scrollTo(0);
        // 关闭按钮
        // patch of getting cookies, since in ie8, when ps is null, returns "undefined"
        if( getPs != 'undefined' && getPs != null && getPs != '' ){ //if(getPs!=null)//getcookie
        // patch end
            $('#closeButton').show().bind('click',function(){
                removeMask();
            });
        } 
        // 关闭按钮end
    }

    // 撤销蒙版，隐藏弹出层
    function removeMask(){
        $('.city_32').hide();
        $('#shadowMask').remove();
    }
    
    // click显示框
    $('.city_cont2_input').bind('click',function(){
        $('.nationwide').show().bind('mouseleave',function(){
            $('.nationwide').hide().find('.nationwide_position').removeClass('nationwide_position');
        });
    });
   
    var timer1 = timer2 = 0;
    // ajax请求地址信息
    function ajaxContent(geoId){
        var geoId = geoId;
        return $.ajax({
                type : "GET",
                url : web_domain+'index.php?r=tGeo/Child',
                data:'geoId='+geoId+'&type='+0,
                timeout: 5000,
                dataType : "jsonp",
                jsonp: 'callback',
                success: function(result){
                    $('.thecity_list').empty();
                    geoData = eval(result);
                    if(geoId == $('.nationwide_position').attr('geoid')){
                        for(x in geoData){
                            $('.thecity_list').append(createContent(geoData[x]));
                        }
                        $('.thecity_list li a').each(function(){
                            $(this).bind('click',function(){
                                cityBindClick.call(this);
                            });
                        });
                        $('.thecity').show().bind('mouseenter',function(){
                           $('.thecity').show();
                           clearTimeout(timer1);
                           clearTimeout(timer2);
                       }).bind('mouseleave',function(){
                           timer1 = setTimeout(function(){$('.thecity').hide();},200);
                       });
                    }
                },
                error: function(){
                    $('.thecity_list').empty();
                }   
            });
        }  


    // 创建地址列表
    function createContent(data){
        var li = document.createElement('li');
        var a = document.createElement('a');
        a.href = "javascript:void(0);";
        $(a).attr('geoId',data.ID);
        $(a).attr('geoLevel',data.LEVEL);
        $(a).attr('substationID',data.SUBSTATION);
        a.href = "javascript:void(0);";            
        a.title = data.NAME;   
        $(a).html(data.NAME);     
        $(li).append($(a));   
        return li;
    }
   
    // 省的市级或直辖市的区级
    function cityBindClick(){
        var geoId = $(this).attr('geoid');
        if(isMu != -1){
            $('#ttcity').attr('cityname',$('#ttprov').attr('provname'));
            $('#ttcity').val(municipalities[isMu].city);
            $('#ttdistinct').attr('distinctname',$(this).html());
            $('#ttdistinct').val(geoId);
            if(typeof geoData[geoId].child != 'undefined'){
                for(var x in geoData[geoId].child){
                    $('#ttarea').attr('areaname',geoData[geoId].child[x].NAME);
                    $('#ttarea').val(geoData[geoId].child[x].ID);
                    break;
                }
            }else{
                $('#ttarea').attr('areaname','');
                $('#ttarea').val(0);
            }
        }else{
            $('#ttcity').val(geoId);
            $('#ttcity').attr('cityname',$(this).html());
            if(typeof geoData[geoId].child != 'undefined'){ 
                for(var x in geoData[geoId].child){
                    $('#ttdistinct').attr('distinctname',geoData[geoId].child[x].NAME);
                    $('#ttdistinct').val(geoData[geoId].child[x].ID);
                    break;
                }
            }else{
                $.ajax({
                    type : "GET",
                    url : web_domain+'index.php?r=tGeo/Child',
                    data:'geoId='+geoId+'&type='+0,
                    timeout: 5000,
                    dataType : "jsonp",
                    jsonp: 'callback',
                    success: function(result){                      
                        for(var x in result){
                            $('#ttdistinct').attr('distinctname',result[x].NAME);
                            $('#ttdistinct').val(result[x].ID);
                            break;
                        }
                        _intoObj.setGeos($('#ttprov').val(), $('#ttcity').val(),$('#ttdistinct').val(),$('#ttarea').val());                       
                    },
                    error:function(){}
                });
            }
            $('#ttarea').attr('areaname','');
            $('#ttarea').val(0);
        }
        $(this).addClass('nationwide_position').parent().siblings().find('.nationwide_position').removeClass('nationwide_position');
        $('.thecity').hide();
        $('.nationwide').hide();
        if(isMu != -1){
            var addr = $('#ttprov').attr('provname')+' '+$('#ttdistinct').attr('distinctname');
            if($('.city_cont2').is(':visible')){
                $('.city_cont2_input').val(addr);
            }
        }else{
            var addr = $('#ttprov').attr('provname')+' '+$('#ttcity').attr('cityname');
            if($('.city_cont2').is(':visible')){
                $('.city_cont2_input').val(addr);
            }
        }
        $('#ttarea').val(0);
        if($('#ttcity').val() == 2){
            for(x in defaultBeijingGeoID){
                if(geoId == x)
                    $('#ttarea').val(defaultBeijingGeoID[x]);
            }
        }      
        _intoObj.setGeos($('#ttprov').val(), $('#ttcity').val(),$('#ttdistinct').val(),$('#ttarea').val());
    }
    // 市级end
    
    // 地址列表切换
    var haveclick = false;
    $('#selectTab').bind('click',function(){
        var obj = $('#selectTab img');
        imgTab(obj);
        $('.city_cont1').toggle();
        $('.city_cont2').toggle();
        $('.thecity').hide();
        $('.nationwide').hide();
        if(haveclick){
            return true;
        }    
        $.ajax({
           type: "GET",
           url: web_domain+'index.php?r=tGeo/getProv',
           data: 'type='+0,
           timeout: 5000,
           dataType: 'jsonp',
           jsonp: 'callback',
           success: function(result){
               haveclick = true;
               $('.nationwide_list').empty();
               for(x in result){
                   var provList = $('.nationwide_list');
                   provList.append('<li><a geoId="'+result[x].ID+'" geoLevel="'+result[x].LEVEL+'" href="javascript:void(0);" title="'+result[x].NAME+'">'+result[x].NAME+'</a></li>');
               }
               // 省级
                $('.nationwide_list li a').each(function(){
                    var t = this;
                    var index = $(t).parent().index();
                    var top = parseInt($('.thecity').css('top'));
                    $(t).bind('click',function(){
                       $('.thecity_list').empty();
                       $('#ttprov').attr('provname',$(t).html());
                       $('#ttprov').val($(t).attr('geoid'));
                       $('.thecity').hide();
                       isMu = isMuni($('#ttprov').val());
                       ajaxContent($(t).attr('geoid'));
                       if(language == 'zh_cn'){
                           var thecityHmlt = "<div class='thecity' style='display:none;'>" + $('.thecity').html() + "</div>";
                           $('.thecity').remove();
                           $(t).parents('li').append(thecityHmlt);
                           $(t).parents('li').addClass('position_city').siblings('.position_city').removeClass('position_city');
                       }else {
                           $('.thecity').css('top',Math.floor(index/3)*26+top+'px');
                       }                               
                       $(t).bind('mouseleave',function(){
                           timer2 = setTimeout(function(){$('.thecity').hide();},200);
                           $(t).unbind('mouseleave');
                       });
                       $(t).addClass('nationwide_position').parent().siblings().find('.nationwide_position').removeClass('nationwide_position');
                   });
                });
            // 省级end
           },
           error: function(){
               
           }
        });

    });
    // 地址列表切换end
    // 图片切换
    function imgTab(obj){
        if(language == 'zh_cn')
            var img = obj.attr('src')=="http://misc.ttmimg.com/images/cn/ticon/city_dn.png"?"http://misc.ttmimg.com/images/cn/ticon/city_up.png":"http://misc.ttmimg.com/images/cn/ticon/city_dn.png";
        else          
            var img = obj.attr('src')=="http://misc.ttmimg.com/images/cn/2013/city_2013_tit.gif"?"http://misc.ttmimg.com/images/cn/2013/city_2013_title.gif":"http://misc.ttmimg.com/images/cn/2013/city_2013_tit.gif";
        obj.attr('src',img);
    }
    // 图片切换end
    // 开始购买
    $('.city_search_r').bind('click',function(){
        var wholeGeo = $('#ttprov').val()+'-'+$('#ttcity').val()+'-'+$('#ttdistinct').val()+'-'+$('#ttarea').val();
        if($('.city_cont2_input').val()=='')
            wholeGeo = '1-2-3-0';// 默认北京东城区
        wholeGeoObj = wholeGeo.split('-');
        _intoObj.setGeos(wholeGeoObj[0],wholeGeoObj[1],wholeGeoObj[2],wholeGeoObj[3],function(){var newUrl = returnReUrl();header(newUrl);});
    });
    // 开始购买end

    // 32城
    $('.city_cont1_list a').each(function(){      
        $(this).bind('click',function(){
            var geo = $(this).attr('geo');
            geoObj = geo.split("-"); //字符分割
            var addre = $(this).html();
            _intoObj.setGeos(geoObj[0],geoObj[1],geoObj[2],geoObj[3],function(){var newUrl = returnReUrl();header(newUrl);});        
        });
    });
    // cuihang
    function returnReUrl(){
        var defaultstation = 1;
        var url = window.location.href;
        var index = '/index-';
        var list  = '/list-';
        var actlistgoods = '/actlist-goods-';
        var actlist = '/actlist-';
        var stationID = _intoObj.getSubStationID();    
        
        var jsonObj = '';
        if(url.indexOf(index) >= 0){
            jsonObj = {"name":"index","station":stationID};
        }else if(url.indexOf(list) >= 0){
            jsonObj = {"name":"list","id":0,"substation":stationID};
        }else if(url.indexOf(actlistgoods) >= 0){
            jsonObj = {"name":"actlist-goods"};
        }else if(url.indexOf(actlist) >= 0){
            jsonObj = {"name":"actlist"};
        }
        //return url;
        if(jsonObj == ''){
            return url;
        }else{    
            var urlCreaterObj = new urlCreater;
            var newUrl = urlCreaterObj.geturl(jsonObj); 
            return newUrl;
        }
    }    
   
});

/*
 * hover handler
 */    
var hover_list= Array();
hover_list[0] = ['.en_top_r2','.en_orders_cont'];
hover_list[1] = ['#myAccountDown','#myAccountMenu'];
hover_list[2] = ['#phoneDown','#phoneMenu'];
var regHover = function(i)
{
    $(hover_list[i][0]).hover(
      function () {
        $(this).children(hover_list[i][1]).show();
        if( $(this).find(".not_used_coupon_count").is(":hidden") ){
            $.ajax({
                type: "GET",
                url : web_user_domain + "index.php?r=tCoupon/ajaxGetCouponCount&type=0",
                dataType:'jsonp',
                timeout: 10000,
                success:function(res){
                    if( res.err_code==0 ){
                        if(res.data!=0 ){
                            $(".not_used_coupon_count").html('('+res.data+')');
                            $("#myAccountMenu .not_used_coupon_count").show();
                            $(".en_orders_cont .not_used_coupon_count").show();
                        }
                    }
                }
            })
        }
      }, 
      function () {
        $(this).children(hover_list[i][1]).hide();
               
      }
    );     
};
for( i=0;i< hover_list.length;i++)
{
    regHover(i);    
}

       $(function(){
        /*
          * 导航分类页跳转
         */     
            var _url = (typeof(_url) !== 'undefined') ? _url : new urlCreater(); 
            $("#nav a[cat]").each(function(i){
                var catID = $(this).attr("cat");
                if(catID == '' || typeof catID == 'undefined')  return;               
                var listUrl = _url.geturl({name:"cat",id:catID});
                $(this).attr('href',listUrl);
            });
          
            var actlistGoodsUrl = _url.geturl({name:"actlist-goods",isNav:1});
            $(".actlistGoods").attr('href',actlistGoodsUrl);

            $(window).scroll(function(){
                    var stop = $(this).scrollTop();
                   var h = $(window).height();
                    if (stop < h) {
                            $('#gotop').fadeOut(500);
                    }
                    else {
                            $('#gotop').fadeIn(500);
                    }
            });
    });
        if($("#zyzy").length >= 1){
                            var zyzy = '#zyzy';
                    }else{
                            var zyzy = '#zyzy1';
                    }

        var start = parseInt($(zyzy+' .forifindexads').attr("starts"));
        var end = parseInt($(zyzy+' .forifindexads').attr("end"));    
        var now = parseInt(new Date().getTime());

    if(now < end && now > start){
     if($(".hidethis").length == 0){
           var film = new Object();
               film.play = function(){
                   $(zyzy+" #littAds").animate({height:"70px"},2000,function(){$(zyzy+" #turnoff").show();}); 
                };

                film.replay = function(){
                    $(zyzy+" #turnoff").hide();
                    $(zyzy+" #littAds").animate({height:"0px"},1500,function(){
                        $(this).hide();  
                    });      
                };                   
                $(document).ready(function(){     
                    setTimeout(function(){     
                        $(".title2014").before($("#zyzy").clone());
                           $(zyzy).show();                                        
                                setTimeout(function(){                                 
                                    film.play();                              
                                },2000);
                     },2000);                   
                });

                $(zyzy+" #turnoff").live("click",function(){
                     film.replay();
                });
            }    
     }
           /*
          * 左侧菜单
         */                            

            $(".tall_menu_list li").mouseenter(function(){          
                var index = $(this).index();
                $(".tall_menu_count").eq(index).show().siblings().hide().parents('.tall_menu_counts').show();
                $(this).addClass('select').siblings().removeClass('select');


                var height = parseInt($(".tall_menu_counts").css('height'));
                var bottom = $(window).height() - ($(this).offset().top - $(document).scrollTop());
                if(height > bottom){
                    var top = $(window).height() - ($(".tall_menu_list").offset().top - $(document).scrollTop()) - $(".tall_menu_counts").height();
                    top = top < 0 ? 0 : top;               
                }else{
                    var top = $(this).position().top;
                }             
                $(".tall_menu_counts").stop().animate({top: top+'px'}, 400);

        });
        $("#hideindex").mouseleave(function(){
            $('.tall_menu_count,.tall_menu_counts').hide();
            $(".tall_menu_list li").removeClass('select');
        });

        var subStationId = _intoObj.getSubStationID();
        var headerStationId = $("#header").attr('substationId') ? $("#header").attr('substationId') : 1;
        changeHeader = false;
        if(subStationId != headerStationId && !changeHeader && (typeof noHeadChange == 'undefined' || !noHeadChange)){
            $.ajax({
                type: "GET",
                url: web_domain + "index.php?r=TCommon/GetHeader&changeHeader=1&lang=" + language + "&stationId=" + subStationId,
                timeout: 15000,
                dataType: "jsonp",
                jsonp: 'callback',
                success: function(data) {
                    changeHeader = true;

                    laterScriptsRun();
                    buyerInfo.load();
                },
                error: function(){
                    //alert('网络异常，请刷新重试');
                }
            });

        }

/*
 * search input keywords
 */    
if ($("#search_input").attr("value")+'' == ""){
    var searchwords = $("#newword").attr("title"); 
    $("#search_input").attr("style", "color:#a8a8a8;font-size:14px;");
    $("#search_input").attr("value", searchwords);
    $("#search_input").click(function (){
        if ($("#search_input").attr("style")+'' != "color:#000;font-size:14px;"){
            $("#search_input").attr("value","");
        }
        $("#search_input").attr("style", "color:#000;font-size:14px;");
    });
}
else {
    $("#search_input").attr("style", "color:#000;font-size:14px;");
}

var HorizSlide = function (new_obj_str){
	this.ads_goods_obj_ls = new Array();
	this.index = 0;
	this.clickLeftStr =  new_obj_str+".clickLeft();";
	this.clickRightStr =  new_obj_str+".clickRight();";
	this.pos_max_no = 4;
	this.initGoodsList = function (pos_max, dom_id, left_button_id, right_button_id){
		var i = 0;
		var obj = this;
		this.step = 1;
		this.dom_id = dom_id;
		this.animate_time = 100;
		this.ads_pos_max = pos_max;
		this.left_button_id = left_button_id;
		this.right_button_id = right_button_id;

		// 这里是干吗的待定？？
		$('#'+ dom_id + ' li').each(function (){
			obj.ads_goods_obj_ls[i++] = this;
		if ($(this).html() == ""){
			obj.step = 2;
		}
		else{
			//alert($(this).html());
		}
		});

		//如果要切换的少于每一屏显示的，则就不用切换了
		if (this.ads_goods_obj_ls.length * this.step <= pos_max){
		    $("#"+this.left_button_id+" a").attr("href", "javascript:;;");
		    $("#"+this.right_button_id+" a").attr("href", "javascript:;;");
		    return;
		}

		for (var i = 0; i < this.ads_goods_obj_ls.length; i += 1){
			if (i >=  this.ads_pos_max * this.step){
				$(this.ads_goods_obj_ls[i]).hide();
			}else{
				$(this.ads_goods_obj_ls[i]).show();
			}                    
		}
		//这个也很纳闷
		if (this.ads_goods_obj_ls.length <  this.ads_pos_max * this.step){
			//alert($(this.ads_goods_obj_ls[this.ads_goods_obj_ls.length]).html());
			$(this.ads_goods_obj_ls[this.ads_goods_obj_ls.length-1]).hide();
		}

		tmpstr = "";
		for(var i = 0; i < pos_max; i++){
			tmpstr += this.clickRightStr;
		}
		this.clickRightStr = tmpstr;
		tmpstr = "";
		for(var i = 0; i < pos_max; i++){
			tmpstr += this.clickLeftStr;
		}
		this.clickLeftStr= tmpstr;
		$("#"+this.left_button_id+" a").attr("onClick", "javascript:"+this.clickLeftStr);
		$("#"+this.right_button_id+" a").attr("onClick", "javascript:"+this.clickRightStr);                                          
	}
	this.clickLeft = function (){
		if (this.index <= 0){
			for(var i = 0; i <=this.ads_pos_max; i++){
				$(this.ads_goods_obj_ls[i]).hide();
			}
			if(this.ads_goods_obj_ls.length%this.ads_pos_max == 0)
				this.index = this.ads_goods_obj_ls.length;
			else{
				this.index = this.ads_goods_obj_ls.length+this.ads_pos_max-(this.ads_goods_obj_ls.length%this.ads_pos_max);
			}
		}      

		this.index -= this.step;//alert( this.ads_goods_obj_ls.length%this.ads_pos_max )
		$(this.ads_goods_obj_ls[this.index]).show();
                
                if (this.step > 1)
                    $(this.ads_goods_obj_ls[this.index + 1]).show();
                $(this.ads_goods_obj_ls[this.index + this.ads_pos_max * this.step ]).hide();
                if (this.step > 1)
                    $(this.ads_goods_obj_ls[this.index + this.ads_pos_max * this.step  + 1]).hide();
                //math.floor() 返回小于或等于指定数字的最大整数
                if (Math.floor((this.ads_goods_obj_ls.length - this.step) / (this.ads_pos_max * this.step))  >= Math.floor((this.index) / (this.ads_pos_max * this.step))){
			$("#"+this.right_button_id+" a").attr("onClick", "javascript:"+this.clickRightStr);                                         
			if (typeof(rightBtnImgEn)!="undefined"){
				$("#"+this.right_button_id+" a img").attr("src",rightBtnImgEn);
			}
                }
			if (0 >= this.index){
				$("#"+this.left_button_id+" a").attr("href", "javascript: ;");
				if (typeof(leftBtnImgUn)!="undefined"){
					$("#"+this.left_button_id+" a img").attr("src",leftBtnImgUn);
				}
				return
			}
	}

	this.clickRight = function (){
		if (Math.floor((this.ads_goods_obj_ls.length - this.step) / (this.ads_pos_max * this.step)) <= Math.floor((this.index) / (this.ads_pos_max * this.step))){
			for(var i = this.index; i <this.ads_goods_obj_ls.length; i++){
			     $(this.ads_goods_obj_ls[i]).hide();
			}
			this.index = -this.ads_pos_max;
		}
		$(this.ads_goods_obj_ls[this.index]).hide();
		if (this.step > 1)
		    $(this.ads_goods_obj_ls[this.index + 1]).hide();
		$(this.ads_goods_obj_ls[this.index + this.ads_pos_max * this.step ]).show();
		if (this.step > 1){
		    if (this.ads_goods_obj_ls.length - this.index - this.step > this.ads_pos_max * this.step){
			$(this.ads_goods_obj_ls[this.index + this.ads_pos_max * this.step  + 1]).show();
		    }
		}
		this.index += this.step;
		if (this.index > 0){
			$("#"+this.left_button_id+" a").attr("onClick", "javascript:"+this.clickLeftStr);                                                                             
		    if (typeof(leftBtnImgEn)!="undefined"){
			$("#"+this.left_button_id+" a img").attr("src",leftBtnImgEn);
		    }
		}
		if (Math.floor((this.ads_goods_obj_ls.length - this.step) / (this.ads_pos_max * this.step)) <= Math.floor((this.index) / (this.ads_pos_max * this.step))){
		    $("#"+this.right_button_id+" a").attr("href", "javascript: ;");
		    if (typeof(rightBtnImgUn)!="undefined"){
			$("#"+this.right_button_id+" a img").attr("src",rightBtnImgUn);
		    }
		    return
		}
	}
}

                }
                else
                {
                     
                    $(this).find(".pro_second_grab").html('<span class="font_gray">'+ttt[4]+'</span>');
                }
            });

      var VisibleSlide = function (linum,dom_id,left,right){
    var move_one_width=parseInt($('.'+ dom_id + ' ul>li').css("width"))+1+parseInt($('.'+ dom_id + ' ul>li').css("margin-left"));//alert(move_one_width)//大图宽度及左侧margin
        var num = parseInt($('.'+ dom_id + ' ul>li').length);//alert(num)
        var slidenum= linum;
        var lock = 1 ;
        var rollright = function(target)
        { 
           if(lock == 2){  return ;}
       
            if(typeof(target)=='undefined')
            {                
                var cu_scroll = parseInt($('.'+ dom_id ).scrollLeft());                                
                target = cu_scroll+slidenum*move_one_width;                                
            }            
            if(target>((num-slidenum)*move_one_width))
            {
                var target=0;
            }     
           
           
            lock =2;
            moveSlowDown(target);
        }    
         var rollleft = function(target)
        { 
           if(lock == 2){  return ;}
       
            if(typeof(target)=='undefined')
            {                
                var cu_scroll = parseInt($('.'+ dom_id ).scrollLeft());                                
                target = cu_scroll-slidenum*move_one_width;                                
            }            
            if(target<-2)
            {
                var target=(num-slidenum)*move_one_width;
            }     
           
           
            lock =2;
            moveSlowDown(target);
        }   
        //#-减速运动效果
        var moveSlowDown = function(target)
        { 
            var ns = target-parseInt($('.'+ dom_id).scrollLeft()); 
            moveElement(ns);        
        }
        //#-减速运动子阶段，递归函数，归零方休
        var moveElement = function(ns)
        {   
            if(ns==0)
            {  
                lock= 1;
                return;
            }
           
            var step=ns>0?parseInt(Math.ceil(ns/10)):parseInt(Math.floor(ns/10));//这里的ceil跟floor的结果，在绝对值上是一样的
           $('.'+ dom_id).scrollLeft(parseInt( $('.'+ dom_id).scrollLeft())+step);
            ns=ns-step;   
            var _moveElement = function(ns)
            {
                return function()
                {
                    moveElement(ns);
                };
            };
            setTimeout(_moveElement(ns),1);  // alert(2)
           // $('#'+left).click(function(){roll();}) ;
        }
        
      
         this.init = function(){
        
             $('#'+left).click(function(){
                 rollleft();
                              
                $('.timg_list_cont').find("img").each(function(){ 
                    var img = this;
                     if(img.getAttribute("initsrc")){       
                               img.src = img.getAttribute("initsrc");
                               img.removeAttribute("initsrc");
                           }
                 });
       
             }) ;
        
             $('#'+right).click(function(){
                 rollright();
                   $('.timg_list_cont').find("img").each(function(){ 
                    var img = this;
                     if(img.getAttribute("initsrc")){       
                               img.src = img.getAttribute("initsrc");
                               img.removeAttribute("initsrc");
                           }
                 });
             })
            
        }
          }

			if(i<max-1){
			    return i+1;
			}else{
			    return 0;
			}
		};

		if (typeof autoSwitch != 'undefined') {
			clearTimeout(autoSwitch);
		}
		var obj = this;
		switchTime = setTimeout(function() {
		$(obj).addClass('select').siblings().removeClass('select');

		$("#screenboard li").eq($('#switcherboard li').index(obj)).css({'opacity': '1'}).siblings().filter(function() {
			return $(this).css('opacity');
		}).animate({'opacity': 0}, outSecond * 1000, function() {
			$(this).css('z-index', '1');
			$("#screenboard li").eq($('#switcherboard li').index(obj)).css('z-index', '2')
		});

		$("#screenboard li").eq($('#switcherboard li').index(obj)).find("img").each(function() {

$(function() {
        var zhixiashi = {1: ['北京', '北京'], 310000: ['上海', '上海'], 120000: ['天津', '天津'], 500000: ['重庆', '重庆']},
        ps = $.cookies.get('ps');
        window["_BFD"] = window["_BFD"] || {};
        _BFD.BFD_INFO = {
            "user_id": (buyerInfo.getIsGuest(true) ? 0 : buyerInfo.BUYER_ID), //网站当前用户id，如果未登录就为0或空字符串
            "page_type": "homepage" //当前页面全称，请勿修改
        };
        if (!ps) {
            _BFD.BFD_INFO.city = ['北京', '北京'];
            baifendian();
        } else {
            var psArr = ps.split('-');
            if (zhixiashi[psArr[0]]) {
                _BFD.BFD_INFO.city = zhixiashi[psArr[0]];
                baifendian();
            } else {
                var geoIds = psArr.slice(0, 2).join('-');
                $.ajax({
                    type: "GET",
                    url: web_domain + 'index.php?r=tGeo/getNameByGeoId',
                    data: 'geoIds=' + geoIds,
                    timeout: 5000,
                    dataType: 'jsonp',
                    jsonp: 'callback',
                    success: function(res) {
                        var name = res.split(' ');
                        _BFD.BFD_INFO.city = name;
                        baifendian();
                    },
                    error: function() {
                        _BFD.BFD_INFO.city = ['北京', '北京'];
                        baifendian();
                    }
                });
            }
        }
        function baifendian(){
            window["_BFD"] = window["_BFD"] || {};
            _BFD.client_id = "Ctest_ttgs";
            _BFD.script = document.createElement("script");
            _BFD.script.type = "text/javascript";
            _BFD.script.async = true;
            _BFD.script.charset = "utf-8";
            _BFD.script.src = (('https:' == document.location.protocol ? 'https://ssl-static1' : 'http://static1') + '.baifendian.com/service/tuotuogongshe/ttgs_home.js');
            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(_BFD.script);
        }
});

 var mxdp_max=$("#screenboard .timg_slide_recomn").length;
 var mxdp_num= $("#screenboard .timg_slide_recomn a").length;
 var i,j;
 j=0;
 for( i=mxdp_num;i<mxdp_max;i++ )
 {
	
	j=j%mxdp_num;
	$("#screenboard .timg_slide_recomn").eq(i).html( $("#screenboard .timg_slide_recomn").eq(j).html()     );
	j++
 }

$(document).ready(function(){  
	var start = parseInt( $("#upads").find('img').attr("starts") );
	var end = parseInt( $("#upads").find('img').attr("end") );    
	var now = parseInt(new Date().getTime());
	var tims = 0;
	var stationID = 1;
	var strCookie = 'indexPopupTimesBeijing';

	if(now < end && now > start)
	{
		var str = getCookie('geos');
		if (str == '' || typeof str == 'undefined' || str == null) {
                    str = defaultGeos;
		}
		stationID = str.split("|")[12]; //字符分割

		if(stationID == 2)
                    strCookie = 'indexPopupTimesShanghai';

		times = getCookie(strCookie);
                //alert(times);

		if(times == false)
		{
                    var timeExceed = 604800;
                    setCookie(strCookie, timeExceed,timeExceed); 

                    $("#upads").find('.up_ads>img').load(function(){
                        var src = $("#upads").find('.up_ads>img').attr('src');
                        if(src.length > 0)
                        {
                            var img = new Image();
                            img.src = src;
                            var wid = parseInt(img.width + 20);
                            var ban = parseInt(wid/2);
                            var syl = "width:"+wid+"px;margin:120px 0 0 -"+ban+"px;";
                            $(".twbox").attr('style',syl);
                            $("#upads").find('#littAds').removeAttr("id");
                        }
                        else
                                $("#upads").remove();
                    });
		}
		else
			$("#upads").remove();
	}
	else
		$("#upads").remove();

	setInterval(function(){$("#salegoodsLeft").click();},5000 );
		
});

//取得cookie    
function getCookie(name)
{    
	var nameEQ = name + "=";    
	var ca = document.cookie.split(';');	//把cookie分割成组    
	for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {    
		var c = ca[i];	//取得字符串    
		while (c.charAt(0)==' ') {	//判断一下字符串有没有前导空格    
			c = c.substring(1,c.length);	//有的话，从第二位开始取    
		}    
		if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) {	//如果含有我们要的name    
			return unescape(c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length));	//解码并截取我们要值    
		}    
	}    
	return false;    
}

//清除cookie    
function clearCookie(name)
{    
	setCookie(name, "", -1);    
}

//设置cookie    
function setCookie(name, value, seconds)
{    
    var date=new Date();  
    date.setTime(date.getTime()+seconds*1000); 
    var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();      
    document.cookie = name+"="+escape(value)+expires+"; path=/";   //转码并赋值    
}

	$("#upads").remove();
});
